外科附骨流注门

　　　　黄帝灵枢经

　　　　　痈疽篇

　　发于股胫，名曰股胫疽，其状不甚变而痈脓搏骨，不急治，三十日死矣。　　【注　此足少阴之毒也。其状不甚变者，毒附于骨而不外发，故皮肤不甚变为痈毒之状也。】[1p]

Collection of Medical Works from Ancient to Present, Volume 368

Surgical Section on Bone and Leaking Qi

Huangdi's Spiritual Pivot Classics

Pus and Abscess Chapter

When it occurs in the thigh and calf, it is called thigh and calf abscess. Its condition does not change much, but the pus grips the bone. If not treated urgently, death will follow in thirty days. [Commentary: This is the poison of the Foot Shaoyin. The condition not changing much indicates that the poison attaches to the bone and does not manifest outwardly, thus the skin does not show signs of an abscess.][1p]

　　　　千金方 【唐　孙思邈】

　　　　　附骨疽

　　凡附骨疽者，以其无破【《外台》作故，】 附骨成脓，故名附骨疽，喜着大节解中；丈夫产妇，喜着(月坒)中；小儿亦着脊背。大人急著者，先觉痛，不得动摇，按之应骨，痛经日便觉皮肉渐急，洪肿如肥状是也。小儿才手近，便大啼呼，即是肢节有痛候也。大人缓者，先觉肌烘烘然，经日便觉痛痹不随。小儿四肢不能动摇，亦如不随状，看肢节解中，若有肌烘烘处，不知是附骨疽，令遍身成肿，不至溃，体皆有青黯。大人亦有不别，呼为贼风风肿，不知是疽也。凡人身体患热，当风取凉，风入骨解中，风热相搏，便成附骨疽。其候嗜眠沉重，忽忽耳鸣。又秋夏露卧，为冷所折，风热伏结而作此疾。急者热多风少，缓者风多热少。不知取风冷，何故而有此疾？由其血盛肌嫩，为风折之，即使凝结故也。[2p]

Thousand Gold Prescriptions
(Tang Dynasty - Sun Simiao)

On Bone Abscess

In the case of bone abscess, it is named so because it does not break, but rather the pus forms in the bone. It commonly appears in the joints of the limbs; in men and postpartum women, it tends to develop in the abdomen; in children, it often occurs on the back. For adults, if it develops quickly, they first feel pain and cannot move. Pressing on the bone will cause increased pain, and over time, the skin and flesh become increasingly tense and swollen, resembling a fatty condition. For a child, if they approach it with their hand, they will start to cry loudly, indicating pain in their joints. Adults with a slower onset will first feel a warmth in their muscles, and after a day, they will have a sense of pain and numbness. Children may be unable to move their limbs, also appearing as if they cannot be moved. Observing the joints, if there are warm spots in the muscles, and one does not recognize it as a bone abscess, it may lead to generalized swelling without breaking, and there can be a bluish darkening throughout the body. Adults may also misidentify it, calling it "wind swelling," unaware that it is an abscess. Whenever a person suffers from heat in the body, seeking coolness from the wind can cause the wind to enter the joints; when wind and heat clash, it results in a bone abscess. The symptoms include drowsiness and a heavy feeling, along with intermittent ringing in the ears. Furthermore, sleeping exposed to dew in autumn or summer can lead to being affected by the cold, causing the wind and heat to congeal, resulting in this illness. In acute cases, heat is prevalent and wind is less, while in chronic cases, there is more wind and less heat. Not knowing how wind and cold contribute to this illness arises from the abundance of blood and softness of muscles, leading to the wind affecting them and causing congestion.[2p]

凡初得附骨疽，即须急服漏芦汤下之，敷小豆散得消，可服五香连翘汤。　　有久痈余疮，败为深疽者，在腨胫间喜生疮，中水恶露寒冻不瘥，经年成骨疽，亦名胻疮。深烂青黑，四边坚强，中央脓血汁出，百药不瘥。汁溃，好肉处皆虚肿，亦有碎骨出者。可温赤龙皮汤，夏月日日洗，冬月四日一洗，青肉多可敷白(艹闾)茹散，蚀去恶肉，可三日敷之，止后长敷家猪屎散，得瘥止。取猪屎烧灰作末如粉，置疮中令满，白汁出吮去，随更敷之，瘥止。若更青肉，复着白(艹闾)茹散如前法，家猪屎散取平复。凡骨疽百疗不瘥者，可疮上以次灸之，三日三夜便瘥。如疮不瘥，瘥而复发，骨从孔中出者，名为骨疽。取先死乌雌鸡一只，去肉取骨，熬焦如炭，取三家牛棓木刮取屑，三家甑箄各一两，皆烧成灰，合导疮中碎骨，当出数片瘥。[3p]

Whenever one first develops a bone ulcer, it is essential to urgently take Luolu soup and consume it. Applying a mixture of mung bean powder can help eliminate the ulcer, and one can also take a decoction of Wuxiang and Lianqiao.

For chronic ulcers that have deteriorated into deep ones, which often arise in the tibia and lead to sores, causing cold and stagnant conditions that prevent healing for years, they may develop into bone ulcers, also known as "sore bones." These ulcers present as deep, rotten, and bluish-black, with firm and strong edges, and yellowish pus and blood exuding from the center, remaining unhealed despite numerous medicines. The discharge may worsen, the surrounding healthy tissue may become swollen and fragile, and fragments of bone may emerge.

In such cases, warm Red Dragon Skin soup is recommended, washing daily in summer and every four days in winter. For abundant unhealthy flesh, one can apply a mixture made with white (wild) lily powder to devitalize the bad tissue, repeating this application over three days. Afterwards, continue with a mixture of pig dung powder until healing is achieved. The ash from burnt pig dung should be ground into a fine powder and packed into the sore until thoroughly filled; when the white juice oozes out, it should be carefully cleaned, and the application changed as necessary until healing is complete.

If unhealthy flesh persists, reapply the white (wild) lily powder as before, accompanied by the pig dung mixture to balance the condition. For stubborn bone ulcers that do not heal despite a hundred treatments, one should apply moxibustion to the ulcer in a sequential manner; doing this for three days and nights can lead to healing. If the sore does not heal or recurs with bone protruding from an opening, it is called a bone ulcer.

In such cases, take a dead female crow, remove the flesh to keep the bones, and char them until they resemble charcoal. Obtain wood shavings from three cows’ horns, about one tael each, and burn them to ash, and then combine them to treat the ulcerated bone, as this will help in healing it.[3p]

　　　　疮疡全书 【宋　窦汉卿】

　　　　　流注证治

　　血溃流注证，多生膏粱形重之人，有此疾者，好食煎炒炙煿糖蜜之类，其疽大者如鸡卵，形象犹如紫李，只肿不红，内串经络之间，流注骨节之内，遍身酸疼，百节疼痛，用内托散加木瓜、白芍、连翘，再服乳香护心散、黄矾丸，外敷围药。当以意消息，切勿执方也。　　小肠流注证，受在心经伏热，结聚成毒也，当用败毒流气饮，再服清心流气饮治之。[4p]

Treatise on Sores and Ulcers
[Song Dynasty - Dou Hanqing]

Treatment of Flowing and Draining Symptoms

Blood sores associated with flowing and draining symptoms frequently occur in those who are heavyset and fond of eating fried, roasted, and sweetened foods. When the sore is large, it may resemble a chicken egg and appear like a purple plum, swollen but not red. It intertwines with the meridians and flows into the bones and joints, causing overall soreness and pain in every joint. For treatment, use an internal powder combined with papaya, white peony, and forsythia, and also take frankincense heart-nourishing powder and alum pills, along with applying a medicinal wrap externally. One should follow the indications cautiously and not rigidly adhere to formulas.

For small intestine flowing and draining symptoms that stem from heat in the heart channel and result in toxic accumulation, one should use "Defeating Toxin Flowing Qi Decoction" and follow up with "Clearing Heart Flowing Qi Decoction" for treatment.[4p]

　　冷漏湿毒流注，此毒或因足痒抓破，有伤汤火风气，或因寒湿流注于足胫，生疮形如牛眼，四畔紫色黑色，常出臭血水，先用三棱针刺周回血出尽后，用金丝膏贴之，呼出毒水腐肉，后以紫金膏贴，看疮已红活，再合隔纸膏贴之。　　气毒流注证，因喜怒不常，饮食失节，气上停食，或因负重努力，伤其经络，宜服蠲毒流气饮、内托千金散、黄矾丸、护心丹。此证乃乘虚感风湿热相结而成，初生一二，渐至于多，及二三五十者，或遍体皆生，先发汗以解风湿，次用参、芪之剂补之，围药姜汁酢调，次服内托千金散大加参、芪，霖雨加苍朮、泽泻。[5p]

Cold leakage and damp poisons can flow and gather; this poison may arise from scratching an itchy foot, leading to injuries from fire and wind. Alternatively, it may stem from cold dampness accumulating in the feet and lower legs, resulting in ulcers resembling cow's eyes, with surrounding purple and black discoloration, often exuding foul blood and water. First, use a three-edged needle to pierce around the wound to drain the blood completely, then apply golden thread ointment to draw out the toxic fluid and rotten flesh. Afterward, apply purple gold ointment, monitoring the ulcer until it reddens and becomes active again, then cover it with a protective paper ointment.

For symptoms of toxic flow, which occur due to irregular emotions, poor eating habits, food stagnation, or straining oneself with heavy loads, damaging the meridians, one should take herbs to dispel toxins and promote the flow of qi, such as the Decoction to Disperse Toxins or the Inner Treasure Thousand Gold Powder, alum pills, and Heart-Protecting Pills. This condition arises from an external invasion of wind, dampness, and heat, initially manifesting as one or two sores, gradually increasing to more, and potentially spreading all over the body. First, induce sweating to relieve wind and dampness, and then use ginseng and astragalus formulas for nourishment. Mix ginger juice and vinegar with the surrounding medicine. Next, take the Inner Treasure Thousand Gold Powder with increased amounts of ginseng and astragalus; during rainy weather, add aster root and alisma.[5p]

　　　　　附骨证治

　　夫附骨痈者，即贴骨痈也，皆附骨贴肉而生，字虽殊而病则一。此证之发，因盛暑身热，贼风入于骨节，与热相搏，复遇冷湿所折。或居劳太过，两足下水，或坐卧湿地，身体虚弱而受寒邪，致风热伏结壅遏，附骨成疽，着大骨节间，其急者，身不得动，按之应骨痛，经日便觉皮肉生急，洪洪如肥状；其缓者，一点酸疼，渐觉长大，行步艰难，以致骨肉不相续。若失治，令身成脓不溃，至死身变青黯，但痛按之至骨，久则结肿，则成瘰疬。其附骨疽久而即肿结脓，以此为异。若治附骨疽，系贼风中之，则病深脓多。凡偏枯挛曲之生，乃附骨疽之渐也。四肢困倦，乍寒乍热，小便赤，大便濇，无汗，须用紫苏、蕲艾、凤仙草煎汤热熨之，使腠理开发，以布拭干，再用干被覆之，烧乳香熏之。如虚甚，随服人参膏，略加附子以助其气，复以艾火攻之，万无不愈者。[6p]

Treatment for Bone Abscess

The bone abscess, also known as an abscess adhering to the bone, arises from attachment to the bone and meat, and while the terms differ, the affliction is the same. This condition emerges due to intense heat from summer, allowing pernicious wind to enter the joints, which clashes with the heat and is then countered by cold and dampness. It may also occur from excessive labor, standing in water, or sitting or lying on damp ground, combined with a weak body that succumbs to cold pathogens, resulting in wind and heat blocking and restraining, leading to the formation of abscesses at the large joints.

In acute cases, movement is impossible, and pressing on the area causes sharp pain deep within the bone. Over the course of days, there is a sensation of urgency in the flesh, swelling significantly. In mild cases, there may be slight soreness which gradually increases, making it difficult to walk, causing disconnection between bone and flesh. If untreated, the body may develop pus without draining, leading to a darkening of the skin and severe pain upon pressure, and over time this can lead to swelling and a transformed state resembling tuberculosis.

If the bone abscess persists, it may swell and develop pus, hence the distinction. When treating a bone abscess, if the malady is rooted in wind, the condition will be severe, with deep and abundant pus. Any signs of withering or cramping signify the gradual onset of a bone abscess. Symptoms include fatigue in the limbs, alternating chills and fever, reddish urine, difficult bowel movements, and absence of sweating.

To treat this, one should use perilla, wormwood, and balsamodendron decoction for hot compresses to open the pores, dry the area, and then cover with a dry blanket, followed by incense burning to aid in recovery. If there is severe weakness, ginseng paste should be taken, with a small addition of aconite to bolster energy, combined with moxa therapy, ensuring recovery without fail.[6p]

　　　　丹溪心法 【元　朱震亨】

　　　　　附骨疽

　　环跳穴痛，防生附骨疽，以苍朮佐黄蘗之辛，行以青皮，冬加桂枝，夏加黄芩，体虚加杜牛膝，以生甘草为使，大料煎，入生姜汁，食前饮之。痛甚者，恐十数贴发不动，少加麻黄一二贴；又不动，恐疽将成，急掘地成坎，以火煅红，沃以小便，赤体坐其中，以席围下体，使热气熏蒸，腠理开，气血畅而愈。　　附骨痈，热在血分之极，初发时以青皮、甘草治之，破后当养血。[7p]

Danxi Heart Method
By Zhu Zhenheng, Yuan Dynasty

For Bone Abscess

When pain occurs at the Huantiao point, take precautions against developing a bone abscess. Use astringent ingredients like Atractylodes (Cang Zhu) combined with bitter Huang Bai, along with QIng Pi to promote circulation. In winter, add Gui Zhi (Cinnamon Twig), and in summer add Huang Qin (Scutellaria). If the body is weak, include Du Niu Xi (Rehmannia) and use fresh Gan Cao (Licorice) to guide the treatment. Prepare a decoction, and add ginger juice before consuming it.

If the pain is severe and persists after several applications, add one or two packets of Ma Huang. If there is still no improvement and the abscess seems imminent, quickly dig a hole to make a basin, heat it until red, and pour urine into it. Sit in it while surrounded by mats to trap the heat and steam, allowing pores to open, promoting circulation, and healing the condition.

For bone abscesses, where heat is extreme in the blood, treat the initial onset with Qing Pi and Gan Cao; after the abscess has ruptured, it is essential to nourish the blood.[7p]

　　　　外科精义 【元　齐德之】

　　　　　论附骨

　　夫附骨疽者，以其毒气深沉附着于骨也。此疾与贼风相类而不同，人不能辨，治之误矣。盖附骨疽者，夏秋露卧为冷折之，风热伏结，附骨成疽。贼风之候，由风邪之气搏于骨节，故其痛深骨髓，遇寒则痛甚。附骨疽痛而不能转，初按之应骨皮肉微急，洪洪如肥状者是也。其贼风皮骨不甚热，而索索恶寒，时复汗出，常欲热熨痛处，即得少宽。其附骨疽初时但痛无时，乍寒乍热而无汗者，经久不消，阴极生阳，寒化为热而溃也。[8p]

Discussion on Bone Abscess

Bone abscess occurs when toxic gas deeply adheres to the bone. This illness resembles the effects of stolen wind, yet it is different; one cannot distinguish between them, leading to errors in treatment. Bone abscess typically develops when one exposes themselves to cold while resting in summer or autumn, where wind and heat become trapped, causing an abscess to form on the bone. The symptoms of stolen wind arise from the wind pathogen impacting the joints, causing deep pain in the marrow; this pain worsens in the cold. Bone abscess is characterized by pain that prevents movement. Initially, upon pressing the area, one may feel slight discomfort in the skin and flesh, resembling a swelling that is thick and full. The bone affected by stolen wind does not feel very hot, but is accompanied by a chilling sensation, and sweating may occasionally occur, leading to a constant desire to heat the painful area for relief. In the early stage of bone abscess, pain is intermittent and may fluctuate between cold and hot sensations without sweating. If it persists without resolution, the cold transforms into heat, ultimately leading to suppuration.[8p]

贼风不治，久而变为挛曲偏枯，所以不同也。认是贼风，则服越婢治风之剂，即得差矣。认是附骨疽，急宜服漏芦汤，或五香连翘散疏下之，次用内消升麻汤，及溻溃膏贴之之类，纵不能消，亦得浮浅。又有缓疽石疽与附骨疽，亦相类而异者。盖缓疽石疽，皆寒气所作，深伏于骨髓之间，有肿与皮肉相似，若疼而坚硬如石，故谓之石疽；缓疽其热缓慢，积日不溃，久乃亦紫黯色，皮肉俱烂，故名曰紫疽。此二者，其治初觉便宜补虚托里温热之剂以取消之。其次调治，临疾制宜，故不复具载。
　　　　医学入门 【明　李梴】[9p]

When the invading wind is not treated, it can become twisted and withered over time, hence the differences. If one recognizes it as an invading wind, then taking the remedy for wind from the book "Yue Bi" will suffice. If it is recognized as a bone abscess, one should promptly take the decoction of reed and possibly use a five-spice lianqiao powder to promote a bowel movement, followed by the internal remedy "Xingma Decoction" and the application of a plaster for sores. Even if one cannot dispel it, some relief can still be achieved.

There are also slow abscesses, like stone abscesses and bone abscesses, which are similar yet different. The slow stone abscess is caused by cold that sinks deeply into the bones and marrow, appearing swollen like flesh, but is hard and painful as stone, hence the name 'stone abscess.' The slow burrowing abscess has a lingering heat, takes days to form without rupturing, and eventually becomes dark purple with decayed flesh, thus named 'purple abscess.' For both types, initial treatment should involve tonifying the deficiency and warming the body to dispel them. Subsequent treatment should be timely and adapted to the illness, thus no further details are provided.[9p]

　　　　　附骨疽

　　贼风，因风邪搏于骨髓，故其痛亦彻骨，遇寒则甚，外证恶寒有汗，痛处常欲热熨，失治变为挛曲偏枯，宜越婢汤主之。　　缓疽石疽，皆寒气伏于骨髓，但缓疽其热缓慢，色紫黯，久则皮肉俱烂；石疽肿与皮肉相似，疼痛坚硬如石。二者初起便宜温热，托里补虚，次乃随证调治。　　外感因露卧风冷寒湿袭深者，初起痛不能转，寒热无汗，经久寒郁为热，便秘者，漏芦饮子主之。有不敢下者，须分经内托汗散。在尻臀者，内托羌活汤，腿内近膝股漫肿木硬者，内托芪柴汤；腿外侧者，内托酒煎汤；左腿外侧漫肿长阔，行步作痛，以手按至骨大痛者，黄连消毒散。通用槟苏散、败毒散。　　内伤厚味，及劳役与酒后乘凉浴水，邪入髀枢，环跳穴左右，积痰瘀血搏成，宜青草苍蘗汤微汗。服此不愈，恐疽将成者，急掘地坑，用火烧红，沃以小便，令患者赤体坐其上，以被席围抱下截，使热气熏蒸，腠理开，气血畅而愈。[10p]

Attached Bone Sore

The "thieving wind" invades the bone marrow, thus its pain penetrates the bones; it worsens with cold. The external symptoms manifest as aversion to cold with sweating, and the painful area often desires heat application. If untreated, it may transform into contracture and atrophy. The remedy is Yuebì decoction.

For "slow sore" and "stone sore," both are due to cold qi lurking in the bone marrow. However, slow sore presents slow heat, dark purple color, and after prolonged duration, both skin and flesh may decay; stone sore appears swollen and resembles skin, with pain as hard as stone. At the onset of both, warming and tonifying treatment is advised, followed by addressing specific symptoms as they arise.

Exterior infections caused by exposure to cold, dampness, or wind lead to the initial inability to move due to pain and a lack of sweating; prolonged cold can turn into heat, leading to constipation, treatable with Loulu Decoction. If there is a fear of evacuating, internal dispersing methods must be applied. For sores in the buttocks, use Qianghuo decoction internally; for swollen, hard areas near the knees, use Qichai decoction; for the outer thigh, use a wine-prepared decoction; for expansive, long-lasting swelling on the left outer thigh, which causes pain upon walking and pressing down to the bone, Huanglian Xiaodu powder is effective.

Universal remedies include Binsu powder and Baidu powder.

For internal injuries from rich foods, labor, and bathing in cool water after drinking, if pathogens invade the hip joints and affect the left and right huan tiao points, resulting in phlegm and blood stagnation, Qingcao Canglian decoction is recommended for mild sweating. If this is ineffective and fears of sores developing arise, urgently dig a pit, heat it with fire, and soak it with urine. The patient should sit bare-bodied over it, wrapped with a mat to contain the heat, allowing the steam to open the pores and achieve smooth circulation of qi and blood for healing.[10p]

　　内伤生冷饮食寒凉药物，血凝于内，饮食如常，活命饮。食少体倦者，六君子汤加当归、藿香。如因劳役伤食，右腿偏肿者，补中益气汤。　　内伤郁怒，肿痛如锥，赤晕散漫，先用活命饮，次用八物汤加柴胡、牡丹皮、山栀。　　内伤劳役，两腿肿痛，寒热食少，此湿痰下注也，补中益气汤加半夏、茯苓、芍药。　　内伤房室，两臀肿硬，二便不通者，肾气丸料加车前子、牛膝煎服，兼用十全大补汤；有寒热者逍遥散。　　附疽初起，宜青皮、甘草节二味煎服，以行其气，或灸熨患处。若脓已成，即用火针，使毒不得内溃，带生用亦无妨，且不痛，又易敛口。　　附骨疽漫肿光色者，用蜂房、蛇蜕、头发灰各等分为末，每三钱酒调服；或神应膏为丸梧子大，每三十丸，温酒下，外仍贴之。已溃者，用平肌散，或狗头骨烧烟熏之。鱼眼疮亦妙。　　腿上一切寒湿疮，用鸽子粪煅过为末，干掺，如燥痛加黄丹少许，桐油调敷。凡痈疽生伏兔穴者，不治。[11p]

Internal injury from cold drinks and food, as well as cold medicines, leads to blood stagnation inside. If one continues to eat as usual and has a slight loss of appetite, administer the Life-Saving Drink. For fatigue and reduced appetite, use Six Gentlemen Decoction with added Dong Quai and Agastache.

If internal injury is due to labor and there is swelling in the right leg, use the Middle Qi Supplementing Decoction.

For internal injury from overwork, with swelling and pain in both legs, insufficient appetite, this indicates damp phlegm accumulation. Utilize the Middle Qi Supplementing Decoction with added Pinellia, Poria, and Peony.

For internal injuries related to sexual activity, with hard swelling in both buttocks and urinary blockage, take Kidney Qi Pills with added Plantago and Achyranthes, and also use the Ten Complete Tonifying Decoction; if there are cold and heat symptoms, use Xiao Yao San.

At the onset of a furuncle, it is advisable to prepare a decoction of Qing Pi and licorice root to promote qi flow, or apply moxibustion to the affected area. If pus has already formed, use a fire needle to prevent the toxin from bursting inside. Using fresh materials is also acceptable, as it causes no pain and helps close the wound.

For chronic bone swelling with a shiny appearance, mix equal parts of bee wax, snake skin, and hair ash into a powder and take three coins with wine; alternatively, form into pills the size of jujube, taking thirty pills with warm wine, while applying externally. If it has already ruptured, use Smooth Muscle Powder or burn dog skulls to produce smoke for fumigation. This method is also effective for fish eye sores.

For all cold and damp sores on the leg, use processed pigeon droppings as a powder to apply dry. If there is severe pain, add a little yellow lead and apply with tung oil. For any boils or abscesses appearing above the rabbit hole, do not treat.[11p]

　　　　　流注

　　流者，行也；注者，住也。或结块或漫肿，皆因素有痰火，或外感风寒，邪气流行，至其痰注之处而发；或内伤郁怒，以致痰火骤发；或内伤房室，阴虚阳气凑袭，逆于肉理而成；或内伤劳役，饮食搏动而发；或跌扑闪挫，一时气逆血凝而成；或产后恶露未尽，复被感伤凝注。多生四肢或胸腹腰臀关节之处，初起宜葱熨法；实者十六味流气饮败毒散，痰痛便秘者古半硝丸；虚者二陈四物汤、托里益气汤、不换金正气散、六君子汤加芎归、补中益气汤加木香枳壳选用，令其自溃自消。若溃久不敛者，纵有表邪，只托里为主，十全大补汤、人参养荣汤、补中益气汤、托里抑青汤、托里益气汤、八味丸，更佐以豆豉饼、琥珀膏，祛散寒邪，补接阳气。脓成以火针破之，内有脓管以药线腐之。若过用寒凉者不治。[12p]

Flow and Accumulation

"Flow" refers to movement; "accumulation" refers to stillness. Whether it forms as a lump or causes general swelling, it is all due to phlegm and fire. This can arise from external factors such as wind and cold, where the pathogenic energy flows to the site of phlegm and causes a reaction; or it can be due to internal emotional injuries, leading to a sudden surge of phlegm and fire; or from internal injuries related to reproductive matters, where a deficiency in yin leads to the invasion of yang energy, counteracting the body's natural processes; or from physical strain, where diet and activity cause disturbances; or from falls and injuries, where sudden obstruction causes stagnation and blood coagulation; or from postpartum convalescence, where retained lochia leads to further emotional distress and accumulation.

It generally occurs in the limbs or joints of the chest, abdomen, waist, and hips. Initially, one should use scallion compresses. For excess conditions, one can use the Sixteen-Flavored Flowing Qi Drink or Eight Herbal Decoction for dispelling toxins; for those with phlegm pain and constipation, the Ancient Half-Scale Pill. For deficiency conditions, one can use Er Chen Decoction, Si Wu Decoction, Tuo Li Yi Qi Decoction, Bu Zhong Yi Qi Decoction with the addition of Chuanxiong and Gui, or Bu Zhong Yi Qi Decoction with Mu Xiang and Zhi Ke, tailored to promote natural resolution. If the condition has long persisted without improvement, even with external pathogens present, focus on Tuo Li as the primary method, using formulas such as Shi Quan Da Bu Decoction, Ren Shen Yang Rong Decoction, Bu Zhong Yi Qi Decoction, Tuo Li Yi Qing Decoction, Tuo Li Yi Qi Decoction, Eight Flavor Pill, supplemented with Dou Chi Cake and Amber Ointment, to dispel cold pathogens and restore yang energy.

If pus forms, it can be punctured with a fire needle, and internal pus channels can be treated with medicinal wires. However, excessive use of cold treatments is contraindicated.[12p]

　　　　薛氏医案 【明　薛己】

　　　　　附骨疽

　　附骨疽，有因露卧风寒，深袭于骨者；有因形气损伤，不能起发者；有因克伐之剂亏损元气，不能发出者；有因外敷寒药，血凝结于内者。凡此皆宜灸熨患处，解散毒气，补接阳气，温补脾胃为主。若饮食如常，先用仙方活命饮解毒散郁，随用六君子汤补托荣气。若体倦食少，但用前汤培养诸脏，使邪不得胜正。若脓已成即针之，使毒不得内侵，带生用针亦无妨。如用火针亦不痛，且使易敛。其隔蒜灸能解毒行气，葱熨法能助阳气，行壅滞，此虽不见于方书，余尝用之大效，其功不能尽述，惟气血虚脱者不应。[13p]

Xuè Shì Medical Case Study
[Ming, Xuè Jǐ]

Bone Abscess

Bone abscess can occur due to exposure to cold winds while lying down, deeply affecting the bones; it can also arise from injury to the body's vital energy that prevents it from resolving; from overuse of depleting medicines that exhaust the original qi and inhibit recovery; or from applying cold medicines externally that lead to blood stagnation internally. For all these cases, it is advisable to apply moxibustion to the affected area to disperse toxic qi, replenish and revive the yang qi, and primarily warm and support the spleen and stomach. If one’s diet remains normal, first use the "Immortal Formula for Reviving Life" to detoxify and resolve stagnation, and then apply "Six Gentlemen Decoction" to nourish and support the vital qi. If one feels fatigued with reduced appetite, simply using the aforementioned decoctions will nurture the internal organs, preventing evil from overpowering the righteous. If pus has already formed, it should be needled to prevent the poison from invading internally; even using a live needle is acceptable. Using a fire needle does not cause pain and facilitates easier closure. Garlic moxibustion can detoxify and promote the movement of qi, while scallion poultices assist the yang qi and relieve stagnation. Although these methods are not found in formula texts, I have experienced significant efficacy from them, and their benefits cannot be fully recounted, but it should be noted that those with deficient qi and blood should not use them.[13p]

　　　　　流注

　　暴怒所致胸膈不利者，调气为主；抑郁所致而不痛者，宜调经脉，补气血；肿硬作痛者，行气和血；溃而不敛者，益气血为主；伤寒余邪未尽者，和而解之；脾气虚，湿热凝滞肉理而然，健脾除湿为主；闪肭瘀血凝滞为患者，和气血，调经络；寒邪所袭，筋挛骨痛，或遍身痛，宜温经络，养血气。　　流注之证，多因郁结，或暴怒，或脾气虚，湿气逆于肉理；或腠理不密，寒邪客于经络；或湿痰，或闪仆，或产后瘀血流注关节；或伤寒余邪未尽为患。皆因真气不足，邪得乘之，故气凝血聚为患也。然此证或生于四肢关节，或生于胸腹腰臀，或结块，或漫肿，或痛或不痛，悉宜用葱熨法，及益气养荣汤，固其元气，则未成者自消，已成者自溃，可全愈也。若不补气血，及节饮食，慎起居，戒七情，而专用寒凉克伐者，俱不治。[14p]

Flow and Confluence

For issues caused by excessive anger leading to chest and diaphragm discomfort, regulating the qi is paramount; for conditions resulting from depression that do not cause pain, it is advisable to balance the meridians and replenish qi and blood; if there is swelling and hardness accompanied by pain, moving qi and harmonizing blood is necessary; if there is ulceration without healing, focus on boosting qi and blood; if remnants of cold damage still persist, harmonize and resolve it; in cases of spleen qi deficiency leading to damp-heat stagnating in the flesh, strengthening the spleen and eliminating dampness is crucial; for patients experiencing pain due to blood stasis from sudden injury, harmonize qi and blood and regulate the meridians; when cold evil strikes causing muscle spasms and bone pain, or pain throughout the body, warming the meridians and nourishing blood and qi is indicated.

The symptoms of flow and confluence often arise from emotional stagnation, whether from excessive anger, spleen qi deficiency, or dampness rebelling against the flesh; or the pores being insufficiently closed, allowing cold evil to invade the meridians; or due to phlegm dampness, or sudden injuries, or postpartum blood stasis affecting the joints; or from residual cold evil not yet resolved. All these stem from insufficient true qi, allowing evils to take advantage, leading to qi stagnation and blood accumulation causing affliction.

These symptoms may manifest in the limbs and joints, or in the chest, abdomen, lower back, or buttocks; they may present as lumps, generalized swelling, with or without pain. It is wholly appropriate to apply scallion compresses and administer restorative qi and nourishing essence decoction to consolidate vital energy. In such cases, those not yet fully developed will dissipate naturally, and those that have formed will break down on their own, potentially leading to full recovery. However, if one does not bolster qi and blood, neglects diet, is careless about daily living, disregards emotional balance, and only resorts to cold and cool treatments, none will achieve recovery.[14p]

若久而不敛，疮口无伤者，宜豆豉饼或附子饼灸之，以祛散寒邪，接补阳气，或外用琥珀膏贴之。若内有脓管，或生瘀肉而不敛者，用针头散腐之自愈。锭子尤效。　　流注之证，或因饮食劳倦，脾胃伤损；或因房劳阴虚，阳气凑袭；或因营气不从，逆于肉理；或因腠理不密，外邪客之；或暴怒伤肝，或郁结伤脾，或湿痰流注，或跌扑血滞，或产后恶露，皆因气血凝滞而成也。或生于四肢关节，或生于胸腹腰臀，或结块，或漫肿，或作痛，皆元气亏损所致，悉宜葱熨，及用益气养荣汤，固其元气，则未成者自消，已成者自溃。若久而不敛，佐以豆豉饼、琥珀膏，祛散寒邪，补接阳气。若内有脓管而不敛者，用针头散腐化之。经云：形伤肿，气伤痛。又曰：真气夺则虚，邪气盛则实。若不补气血，节饮食，慎起居，戒七情，而专用寒凉克伐，其不死者幸耳。
　　　　医林集要 【明　王玺】[15p]

If there is a wound that does not heal over time, and the wound is not injured, it is advisable to use fermented soybeans or aconite cakes for moxibustion to dispel cold evil and replenish yang energy; or to apply amber ointment externally. If there are internal pus tubes or if there is excess flesh that does not heal, use a needle to disperse the necrotic tissue for self-healing. The use of a pill is particularly effective.

Regarding the symptoms of flowing and swelling, they may arise from dietary indulgence, exhaustion, damage to the spleen and stomach; from excessive sexual activity leading to yin deficiency and an assault on yang energy; from the nourishing energy not following through and reversing within the flesh; from looser pores allowing external evil to invade; from rage damaging the liver; from accumulated stresses harming the spleen; from damp phlegm causing swelling; from trauma causing blood stagnation; or from postpartum lochia. All of these are due to stagnation of qi and blood. These can arise in the limbs and joints, or in the chest, abdomen, waist, and hips; they may present as lumps, diffuse swellings, or pain, all caused by deficit of original qi. It is advisable to use green onion poultices, along with nourishing qi and essence soup to secure the original qi. This will allow what has not fully formed to dissipate naturally, and what has formed to rupture on its own.

If there is a prolonged lack of healing, additionally use fermented soybeans and amber ointment to dispel cold evil and replenish yang energy. If there are internal pus tubes that do not heal, use a needle to disperse and dissolve them. The classics state: when the form is injured, swelling occurs; when the qi is injured, pain arises. It is also stated: if true qi is lost, there is deficiency; if evil qi is excessive, there is fullness. If one does not replenish qi and blood, regulate diet, take care in daily life, avoid the seven emotions, and exclusively use cold and cool remedies, then those who do not perish are merely fortunate.

— Medical Forest Collection Essentials, Ming Dynasty, Wang Xi[15p]

　　　　　附骨疽

　　附骨疽，乃流注之败证也。如用凉药，则内伤其脾，外冰其血。脾主肌肉，脾气受伤，饮食必减，肌肉不生；血为脉络，血受冰则气血不旺而愈滞。宜用理脾脾健则血自生而气自运行矣。　　又有白虎飞尸，留连周期，或展转数岁，冷毒朽骨，出尽自愈。若附骨腐者可痊，正骨腐则为终身废疾矣。有毒自手足或头面肿起，或兼疼痛，上至颈项骨节去处，如瘰疬贯珠，此风湿流气之证也，宜以加减小续命汤及独活寄生汤治之。　　有两膝肿痛起，或至遍身骨节疼痛者，此风湿痹，又名历节风，宜附子八物汤治之。　　又有结核在项腋，或两乳旁，或两胯软肉处，名曰(疒其)疬痈，属冷证也。　　又有小儿宿痰失道，致结核于颈项臀髆胸背之处，亦冷证也，俱宜热药敷贴。　　以上诸证，皆缘于肾。肾主骨，肾虚则骨冷而为患也。所谓骨疽皆起于肾，亦以其根于此也。故用大附子以补肾气，肾实则骨有生气，而疽不附骨矣。[16p]

Appendicular Bone Abscess

The appendicular bone abscess is a sign of the failure of flowing energy. If cool herbs are used, they will internally damage the spleen and externally cool the blood. The spleen governs the muscles; if the spleen qi is harmed, appetite will decrease, and muscles will not grow. Blood is the network of vessels; if the blood is cooled, then the qi and blood will not be abundant and will stagnate. It is advisable to regulate the spleen; when the spleen is healthy, the blood will naturally generate, and the qi will run smoothly.

Furthermore, there is the phenomenon of the white tiger flying corpse, lingering for cycles, sometimes lasting several years, where cold toxins decay the bones, eventually resulting in self-healing. If the bone becomes corrupted, it may recover, but if the bone truly rots, it leads to lifelong disability. Toxic swellings may arise from the hands and feet or head and face, accompanied by pain, extending to the neck and joints, like scrofula with pearls—this is a sign of wind and dampness blocking energy, and should be treated with modified Xiao Xu Ming Decoction and Du Huo Ji Sheng Decoction.

There may also be swelling and pain in the knees, or pain in various joints throughout the body—this is called wind-damp bi, also known as rheumatic wind, and should be treated with Aconite and Eight Ingredients Decoction. Additionally, tubercles may appear in the neck, armpits, near the breasts, or in the soft flesh around the hips, referred to as "disease lesions" and associated with cold conditions.

In children, stagnation of phlegm may lead to tubercles in the neck, buttocks, chest, and back, which is also a cold condition, and should also be treated with warm herbs applied topically.

All of these symptoms arise from the kidneys. The kidneys govern the bones; when the kidneys are deficient, the bones become cold and problematic. The so-called bone abscesses originate from the kidneys, as they have their root here. Therefore, using large Aconite to supplement kidney qi will ensure that when the kidneys are robust, the bones will be vital, and abscesses will not attach to the bones.[16p]

　　　　证治准绳 【明　王肯堂】

　　　　　附骨疽

　　或问附骨疽何以别之？曰：凡患流注，表未尽则余毒附骨而为疽，在股外属足太阳阳明经，在股内属足厥阴足少阴经。又云：风湿折热，热结而附骨成疽。盖骨者肾之余，肾虚则骨冷，而遂附着于骨也。骨冷则气愈滞而愈积，但能为肿不能为脓。流注者伤寒之余毒，骨疽者流注之坏证也。流注非伤寒之罪，乃医者表之未尽也；骨疽非流注之过，乃庸医凉药之误也。又云：久得厚味，乃醉后涉水，或履冰霜雪，寒入髀枢，积痰瘀血相搏而成疽。初时暂痛无时，乍寒乍热而无汗，久则痛深入骨而不移，按之痛不止者，是也。[17p]

Proof of Treatment Guidelines
(Ming - Wang Kengtang)

Affiliated Bone Carbuncle

Someone asked how to distinguish an affiliated bone carbuncle. It is said: In cases of flowing pain, if the exterior is not fully resolved, residual toxins adhere to the bone and form a carbuncle. For those on the outer thigh, it belongs to the Yangming meridian of the foot, while those on the inner thigh belong to the Jueyin and Shaoyin meridians of the foot. Furthermore, it is stated: Wind and dampness, together with heat, lead to heat accumulation that adheres to the bone, resulting in carbuncles. The bone is associated with the kidneys; if the kidneys are deficient, the bones become cold, causing toxins to adhere to them. When bones are cold, qi becomes increasingly stagnant and accumulates, which can result in swelling but not pus. Flowing pain stems from the residual toxins of a febrile disease, whereas bone carbuncles are a complication of flowing pain. The flowing pain is not a fault of the febrile disease but rather an inadequacy in treatment by the physician. Bone carbuncles are not merely a consequence of flowing pain but rather an error by the inept physician in using cooling medicines. Additionally, it is mentioned: prolonged indulgence in rich foods, followed by drunkenness, exposure to water, or walking on ice or snow can lead to cold entering the hip joint, with phlegm and blood stasis interacting to form a carbuncle. Initially, there may be intermittent pain, fluctuating between cold and heat without sweating. Over time, the pain deepens into the bone and is persistent, with continuous tenderness upon pressure; this is the condition.[17p]

初觉即隔蒜灸之，以多为上，宜胜金丹乌金散汗之；壮实者，一粒金丹下之，或八阵散。久则极阴生阳，寒化为热，肉腐而成脓，脓成则宜烙，十全大补汤加牛膝、木瓜补之。有久溃毒结，留连展转，经岁不已，腐出朽骨者，骨虽出而不愈，有终身之咎。视其白脓清稀者，碎骨初脱，肉深难取；脓白而稠者，碎骨将出，肉浅可取。大抵久腐出骨，不论强弱老幼，必须补益，使气血和畅，正气渐复，邪气渐退，自然收敛，十全大补汤、人参养荣汤，在所当用。未成脓者，以冲和膏贴之，盖有独活能动荡气血也。已溃者，宜服何首乌散，此药能调和阴阳也。[18p]

At the initial stage, one should use garlic moxibustion; using more is better. It is essential to overcome the effects of the golden elixir and black gold powder that induce sweating. For those who are robust, one can take a single golden elixir or Eight-array Powder. If it continues for a long time, extreme yin generates yang, cold transforms into heat, leading to rotting flesh and forming pus. When the pus is formed, it is advisable to apply cauterization, supplemented by the Ten Perfectly Nourishing Decoction with added ligusticum and papaya for nourishment.

If there are long-standing toxic accumulations that linger and twist for over a year, resulting in rotten bones; even if the bones emerge, they do not heal and may lead to lifelong consequences. Observe whether the pus is white and thin: this indicates initial bone fragmentation and deep flesh is hard to extract; if the pus is white and thick: this indicates that the bone is about to emerge, and shallow flesh is easier to take. Overall, when long-term decay leads to bone exposure, regardless of strength, age, or weakness, one must provide nourishment to ensure that qi and blood flow harmoniously, restoring proper energy gradually, while dispelling evil energies naturally. The Ten Perfectly Nourishing Decoction and Ginseng Nourishing Decoction should certainly be used.

If pus has not formed, apply a harmonizing ointment because Duhuo can indeed invigorate the movement of qi and blood. If there is already an ulcer, it is advisable to take He Shou Wu Powder, as this medicine can harmonize yin and yang.[18p]

　　　　　流注

　　色黄不串流者，俗曰马(疒其)；串流者名曰走散流注，俗曰瓜藤马(疒其)。外形微肿，骨节内疼甚，名曰嗍骨马(疒其)。若遍身骨节内疼痛不能起坐，无堆，作热不退者，亦曰嗍骨马(疒其)。若脊背及髀骨上起堆，或一二个或三五个，名曰过脊马(疒其)。若尾骶上起堆作热者，名曰杀着马(疒其)。若髁骨下痛甚无堆但肿者，名曰锁脚马(疒其)。若骨相交接之处，疼痛无堆微肿，名曰接骨马(疒其)。此证因风热走散四肢，治当疏风散热。初起不可用火针烙之，肿势盛者只宜刺以棱针，久熟者可火针烙之。流注入股者死。伤寒余邪未尽者和解之，以人参败毒散，次以小柴胡合二陈汤，加羌活、川芎、枳壳、当归、白朮。[19p]

Flowing Injection

If the discoloration is yellow and does not flow, it is commonly referred to as "horse sickness." If it flows, it is called "wandering flowing injection," commonly known as "tendon horse." The external shape is slightly swollen, with severe internal pain at the joints, known as "sucking bone horse." If there is pain in all the joints of the body, preventing one from sitting or standing, with no lumps and persistent heat, it is also referred to as "sucking bone horse." If there are lumps appearing on the spine and hip bones, whether one or two or three to five in number, it is called "over spine horse." If there are lumps with heat on the tailbone, it is called "overstraining horse." If there is severe pain below the knee joint without lumps but with swelling, it is known as "locked foot horse." If there is pain at the joints where bones intersect, with slight swelling but no lumps, it is called "joint bone horse." This condition is due to wind and heat scattering through the limbs; treatment should focus on dispersing wind and relieving heat. Initially, do not use fire needles to cauterize; if swelling is severe, only puncture with a sharp needle. For chronic cases, cauterization with fire needles is acceptable. A flowing injection into the thigh is fatal. If remnants of cold damage remain, harmonization should be applied using Shen Qi Bai Du San, followed by Xiao Chai Hu Tang combined with Er Chen Tang, adding Qiang Huo, Chuan Xiong, Zhi Ke, Dang Gui, and Bai Zhu.[19p]

暴怒所致，胸膈不利者，调气为主，宜方脉流气饮。抑郁所致而不痛者，宜调经脉，补气血，益气养荣汤。肿硬作痛者，行气和血，宜疮科流气饮。溃而不敛者，益气血，宜人参养荣汤、十全大补汤。脾气虚，湿热凝滞肉理而致者，但肿一块不痛，肉色不变，饮食少思，宜健脾除湿，六君子汤加芎、归、黄芪、白芍、肉桂。闪肭瘀血，凝滞为患者，和气血，调经络，宜方脉流气饮，次以二陈合四物，加香附、乌药、桔梗。寒邪所袭，筋挛骨痛，或遍身痛，宜温经络，养气血，宜大防风汤及五积散合败毒散加川牛膝、杜仲，或独活寄生汤；次以四物汤加黄芪、羌活、杜仲。病尚有潮热者，里有寒，邪未尽散，宜荣卫返魂汤加干葛、升麻、紫苏、川芎、独活，姜水煎服。[20p]

For anger causing chest discomfort, focus on regulating the qi, and it is advisable to use the "Flowing Qi Drink." For depression without pain, regulate the vessels, tonify qi and blood with "Tonifying Qi and Nourishing Vitality Decoction." For swelling and hard pain, move qi and harmonize blood; "Sore Department Flowing Qi Drink" is recommended. If it ulcerates and does not heal, tonify qi and blood with "Ginseng Nourishing Vitality Decoction" or "Ten Complete Great Tonifying Decoction." For spleen qi deficiency, with damp heat stagnating the flesh leading to a lump that does not hurt, where the color of the flesh remains unchanged and appetite is low, strengthen the spleen and eliminate dampness using "Six Gentleman Decoction" plus Chuanxiong, Angelica, Astragalus, White Peony, and Cinnamon. For hernia and stasis due to blood coagulation causing the patient pain, harmonize qi and blood, adjust the meridians, using "Flowing Qi Drink," followed by "Erchen Decoction" combined with "Siwu Decoction" plus Cyperus, Lindera, and Platycodon. For cold evils attacking, causing muscle spasms and bone pain, or pain throughout the body, warm the meridians and nourish qi and blood with "Great Danger-Preventing Decoction" combined with "Five Accumulations Powder" and adding achyranthes and eucommia, or "Duhuo Jisheng Decoction"; also consider "Siwu Decoction" with Astragalus, Qianghuo, and Eucommia. If the illness still shows tidal fever indicating lingering cold, suggesting that the pathogen has not entirely dispersed, use "Nourishing Wei and Returning Soul Decoction" with dried kudzu, cimicifuga, perilla, Chuanxiong, and Duhuo, prepared in ginger water for drinking.[20p]

如无潮热，用荣卫返魂汤加独活，酒水各半煎服。接骨马(疒其)，用穿山蜈蚣、白田柯、石楠藤、山良姜、九节香、紫金皮、含笑叶煎水，时时热淋洗之，却服续骨散、九金六马散。起堆核数枚，但小些，名马疔，又名马铃，用紫金锺、紫金皮、紫河车、天南星磨酢暖涂，又用紫金皮、紫金藤、红内消、马蹄香、马蹄藤煎酒服。锁脚马(疒其)，用野芋子根、马蓝草、藜芦子、紫河车、山枇杷根皮、山布瓜根、紫金皮捣烂，盐糟炒敷，又以煎水热淋洗之，却服轻脚散、九金六马散。嗍骨马(疒其)，用穿山蜈蚣、紫金皮、石楠藤、白田柯、溪枫根、九节香、对节金惊煎水淋洗，却服嗍骨散、九金六马散、四味浸酒方。[21p]

If there is no heat or dampness, use Rongwei Reviving Decoction with Du Huo, boiled with equal parts of wine and water. For broken bones, use mountain centipede, white field shell, stone rattan, mountain ginger, nine-segmented incense, purple golden skin, and magnolia leaves to make a decoction, and apply it hot frequently. Afterward, take Continuous Bone Powder and Nine Gold Six Horse Powder. Prepare several small almond-sized kernels, called horse abscess or horse bell, and use purple golden bell, purple golden skin, purple river cars, and tian nanxing, ground with vinegar for warm application, along with purple golden skin, purple golden rattan, red internal eliminates, horse hoof fragrance, and horse hoof rattan decocted in wine for consumption.

For locked feet (neuropathic), use wild yam root, horse blue grass, li lu seeds, purple river cars, mountain loquat root skin, mountain bud gourd root, and purple golden skin, crushed and sautéed with salt, then applied. Additionally, wash with heated decoction and take Light Foot Powder and Nine Gold Six Horse Powder. For bone sucking (neuropathic), use mountain centipede, purple golden skin, stone rattan, white field shell, stream maple root, nine-segmented incense, and twisted golden surprise for a decoction to wash, then take Bone Sucking Powder, Nine Gold Six Horse Powder, and the Four Flavor Immersion Wine formula.[21p]

过脊马(疒其)，用山枇杷根皮、藜芦子、小樟子根皮、天门冬、天南星、仙人掌根、山布瓜根、赤牛膝、半夏、凌霄根皮、佛桑花、马蓝草、野芋子根、天铜柯、普营子根皮、赤毛桃根皮、赤芎根皮捣烂，半泔半酢调，暖刷渣封，瓜藤马(疒其)并效；却服蠲脊散、九金六马散。瓜藤马(疒其)，用山布瓜根多、赤葛子根皮、樟柳根、紫金皮、紫金锺、落鸦枪根、七叶杨香、天花粉、真珠帘根、白芙蓉叶、凌霄根皮、溪枫根皮、赤毛桃根皮捣烂，盐糟炒敷之。又方：山布瓜根、葛合根、紫河车、藜芦子、马鞭穗、紫金皮、山枇杷根皮、凌霄根皮、佛桑花、落鸦枪根、白田柯捣烂，盐糟炒敷之。又方：山布瓜根、紫金皮、溪枫根皮捣烂，酒炒敷之，此方马(疒其)并大效，却服九金六马散、四味浸酒方，又用洗肿方热淋之。[22p]

For the treatment of 'Guati Ma' (a term referring to a health issue), use the roots and peels of various herbs: mountain loquat, Chuanxiong, small zhang (Cinnamomum), Asparagus, Tian Nansheng, cactus, mountain vegetable gourd, red cow knee, pinellia, root bark of the mirabilis, mulberry flower, horse bluegrass, wild taro root, Tian copper branch, root bark of Wuyingzi, red peach root bark, and red xiong root bark. Crush them, mix with half vinegar and half water, warm and apply as a poultice, along with the 'Guati Ma' treatment. Additionally, take 'Juanji San' and 'Jiujin Liuma San.'

For 'Guati Ma,' use a higher quantity of mountain vegetable gourd root, red gezi root bark, camphor willow root, purple gold peel, purple gold trunk, crow's gun root, seven-leaf fragrant herb, tianhuafen (flower), pearl curtain root, white hibiscus leaves, mirabilis root bark, and stream maple root bark. Crush and apply after frying with salt. Another formula consists of mountain vegetable gourd root, gege root, purple river charioteer, licorice seeds, horse whip ear, purple gold peel, mountain loquat root peel, blood mulberry flower, crow's gun root, and white field branch, also crushed and applied after frying with salt. One more formula calls for mountain vegetable gourd root, purple gold peel, stream maple root bark crushed and then cooked in wine for application. This approach for 'Guati Ma' is highly effective. Additionally, take 'Jiujin Liuma San' and 'Four-Flavor Soaked Wine Formula,' and also use the swelling wash and heat topical application.[22p]

杀着马(疒其)，用紫河车、山枇杷根皮、藜芦子、山布瓜根、凌霄根皮、佛桑花、葛合根、石萍捣烂，酢调刷渣封，用洗肿方淋洗，却以九金六马散、蠲骶散服之。诸马(疒其)，有热者用去热散，有表者用荆防败毒散，有里者用内疏黄连汤，有表复有里者用追疔夺命汤；却用水金凤捣烂，敷堆核上即效。马(疒其)有热未成，服药即能退之；若已成者，但要出脓，其热即退。若生堆核四五个，只一二个未成脓，余者皆已出脓，其热亦不能退，要五个尽出脓，热方退也。若溃烂者，即系溃疡，宜查本门治之。　　流注起于伤寒，伤寒表未尽，余毒流于四肢经络，濇于所滞而后为流注也。如病尚有潮热，则里有寒，邪未尽散，荣卫返魂汤，方中可加升麻、苏叶。[23p]

To treat the horse disease (inflamed area), use purple river vehicle, mountain loquat root skin, licorice seeds, mountain cucumber root, climbing vine root skin, Buddhist mulberry flowers, kudzu root, and stone moss, all crushed and mixed with vinegar to create a paste for sealing. Wash the swelling with the prescribed wash, and then take the Nine Gold Six Horse Powder and Jue Di San. For horses with the disease, if there is heat, use the heat-clearing powder; if there are exterior signs, use the Jingfang Baidu powder; if it's internal, use the internal clearing Huanglian Decoction; and if both exterior and internal signs are present, use the Zhua Ding Duo Ming Soup. Crush the Water Jin Feng and apply it to the kernel for effect. If the horse has heat that hasn't fully formed, administering the medicine can reduce it; if it has already formed, it is necessary for the pus to be expelled for the heat to dissipate. If there are four to five kernels present and only one or two have not formed pus while the others have, the heat cannot subside until all five have expelled pus. If it has ulcerated, it is considered an ulcer, and one should investigate and treat it at the source.

Fluid retention originates from cold damage, with lingering toxins flowing into the limbs and meridians, stagnating before leading to the fluid retention. If the patient still has intermittent fever, it indicates internal cold, and the pathogen has not been fully dispersed. The Rong Wei Fan Hun Decoction can be modified with the addition of Sheng Ma and Su Ye.[23p]

如服此而热不退可加干葛，如有头疼加川芎，并用姜水煎。如无潮热，可用水酒相半煎，酒大能行血生气故也。气生血行，病愈可必。然流注须表者何也？所以推其因，究其源，不忘病之根本也。寒邪既尽，表之太过，则为冷流注，尤为难治，故宜略表为妙。表后第二节，宜服温平之药，乃十宣内补是也。如不效，第三节，宜加附子，或服四柱散数服即止。温药亦不可多用，恐增痛苦，反成脓血不干，第四节，仍归本方收效。然表未尽，则余毒附骨而为骨痈。夫流注者，伤寒之余毒；骨痈者，又流注之败证也。流注非伤寒之罪，乃医者表之未尽也。骨痈非流注之过，又庸医凉药之过也。庸医无识，心盲志聋，妄称明见，虽知为骨痈，而治之无法，又复托之凉药，烈之毒刃，则毒气滞，凉药触铁器则愈附骨而不能愈矣。[24p]

If after taking this, the heat does not subside, you may add dry kudzu. If there is a headache, add Chuanxiong and boil it with ginger water. If there is no damp-heat, you may boil it with half water and half wine, as wine can promote blood circulation and vital energy. When energy circulates, blood flows, and recovery is assured. However, why should we address the surface issues? This is to trace the cause, explore its origins, and not forget the root of the illness. Once the cold evil is eliminated, if the surface treatment is excessive, it leads to cold retention, which is particularly difficult to treat, so a slight surface treatment is preferable.

After the surface treatment, in the second stage, it is advisable to take warm, neutral medicines, which essentially serve to replenish the interior. If this is ineffective, in the third stage, you should add Aconite or take the Si Zhu San for a few doses and then stop. Warm medicines should also not be overused, for fear of increasing suffering, which might turn into pus or blood that cannot be resolved. In the fourth stage, revert to the original formula to achieve results. However, if the surface condition is not resolved, lingering toxins may attach to the bones, leading to bone abscesses.

Flowing retention is the residual toxin from cold damage; bone abscesses are the failed manifestations of flowing retention. Flowing retention is not the fault of cold damage but rather the result of inadequate surface treatment by the physician. Bone abscesses are not simply a consequence of flowing retention, but also the fault of incompetent doctors who use cold medicines improperly. Incompetent doctors lack insight, are blind in mind and deaf in spirit, and falsely claim to have clear perception. Even if they recognize bone abscesses, they have no effective methods to treat them, relying instead on cold medicines and harsh toxic treatments, causing toxin stagnation. Cold medicines, when they encounter iron utensils, further attach to the bones and cannot resolve the issue.[24p]

不然，则人之骨何以有痈？骨而成痈，非药所治，故名附骨疽，又名曰虎飞尸。留连周期，展转数岁，冷毒朽骨，出尽自愈。其不愈者，至于终身有之，此皆失于初也。其骨腐者，多为副骨，犹或可痊，正骨腐则终身废疾。故脓白而清者，碎骨初脱，肉深难取；脓黄而稠者，碎骨将出，肉浅可取，宜以利刃取之。　　又有流注大如匏瓠覆碗，见于胸背，其证类发而甚，用荣卫返魂汤之后，形势一有微动，即非发矣，宜以内补十宣，与此方随证通变用之，可以内消。大抵流注皆原于冷，故为痛者骨痛也，骨者肾之余，肾虚则骨冷，骨冷所以痛，所谓骨疽皆起肾者，亦以其根于此也。故补肾必须大附子，方能作效。肾实则骨有生气，疽不附骨矣。凡用药不可执一，贵乎通变。　　流注冷证，多附骨内，硬不消，骨寒而痛，筋缩不伸。[25p]

Otherwise, how could the bones of a person have abscesses? When bones form abscesses, they cannot be treated with medicine, hence they are called "bone-attach abscess" and also "tiger-flying corpse." If it lingers for a while, extending over several years, the cold poison decays the bone, and it may eventually heal by itself. Those that do not heal may persist for a lifetime; this is a failure from the outset. Many instances of bone decay involve accessory bones, which may still heal, but decay of the main bones results in lifelong disabilities. Therefore, when the pus is white and clear, it signifies that the shattered bone has just come loose, and the flesh is deep and difficult to extract; when the pus is yellow and thick, it means the shattered bone is about to come out, and the flesh is shallow and easier to access, thus it is advisable to use a sharp blade for extraction.

There are also cases of fluid accumulation as large as a gourd covering a bowl, seen on the chest or back, whose symptoms are similar to a fever; after using the nourishing and circulating herbal decoction, if there is even a slight change in condition, it is no longer a fever. It is suitable to use internal supplements as complementary treatments, with variations according to symptoms, to help eliminate the interior issues. Generally, fluid accumulation originates from cold, hence the pain is in the bones; the bones are a residue of the kidneys, and when the kidneys are deficient, the bones become cold, causing pain, as what is called "bone abscess" arises from kidney issues, rooted in this fact. Therefore, to nourish the kidneys, one must use great aconite to achieve the desired effect. When the kidneys are robust, the bones are vitalized, and abscesses do not attach to the bones. In all medicinal applications, one should not adhere to a single way, but rather value adaptability and change.

For cold conditions of fluid accumulation, it largely attaches within the bones, becoming hard and unyielding, with cold bones causing pain, and muscles unable to stretch or extend.[25p]

若轻用刀针，并无脓血，若止有乳汁清流，或有瘀血，宜用此药敷之。若稍缓，止以军姜、白芷、肉桂、草乌等分，热酒调敷，骨寒除而痛止，则气温和而筋自伸，肉硬自消矣。然治流注不可无木蜡以破积滞之气，消坚硬之肿，最妙。又不可多，多则能解药性，盖此证主于温药故也。　　或问足胫之间生疮，状如牛眼，或紫或黑，脓水淋漓，止处即溃烂，久而不敛，何如？曰：此名湿毒流注，暴风疾雨，寒湿暑气，侵入腠理而成，宜防风通圣散加木瓜、牛膝、防己之类，或当归拈痛汤加牛膝。　　或问脚膝间脓水不绝，连年不愈，何如？曰：此名下注疮，亦名湿毒疮。因脾胃湿热下注，以致肌肉不仁而成疮也。在外属足太阳少阳经，在内属足厥阴足太阴经。宜服防风通圣散加木瓜、防己、牛膝之类，外用祛风等汤药洗，制女贞叶贴之。[26p]

If there is light use of knives or needles and no pus or blood, but only a clear flow of milk-like liquid, or if there is stagnant blood, this medicine should be applied. If the symptoms ease slightly, mix equal parts of military ginger, white angelica, cinnamon, and black grass, adjusting with hot wine for application; this will relieve cold in the bones and stop pain, leading to warmth in the qi, allowing the muscles to naturally stretch, and hard flesh to dissipate. However, when treating flowing and festering conditions, one must not be without wood wax to break the stagnant qi and dissolve hardened swellings which is most effective. But do not use too much, as excess can neutralize the medicinal properties, since this condition primarily requires warming medicines.

If asked about sores between the legs that resemble a cow's eye, either purple or black, with pus flowing profusely and decaying at the edges without healing for a long time, one should say: This is called damp toxin flowing sores; caused by violent winds and sudden rains that invade the pores and lead to this condition. It should be treated with a Fengfeng Tongsheng Powder combined with papaya, achyranthes, and the like, or with a Danggui Nian Pain Decoction with added achyranthes.

If asked about continuous pus between the knees that has not healed for years, one might say: This is referred to as lower sores, also known as damp toxin sores. This arises from damp heat in the spleen and stomach descending, leading to numbness in the muscles, resulting in sores. Externally, it belongs to the foot's Taiyang and Shaoyang channels, while internally it belongs to the foot's Jueyin and Taiyin channels. It is advisable to take Fengfeng Tongsheng Powder with papaya and the like, while externally using decoctions to dispel wind for washing, and applying leaves of the female privet.[26p]

　　　　外科正宗 【明　陈实功】

　　　　　附骨疽

　　夫附骨疽者，乃阴寒入骨之病也。但人之气血生平壮实，虽遇寒冷则邪不入骨。凡入者，皆由体虚之人，夏秋露卧，寒湿内袭，或房欲之后，盖覆单薄，寒气乘虚入里，遂成斯疾也。初起则寒热交作，稍似风邪，随后臀腿筋骨作痛，不热不红，疼至彻骨，甚者屈伸不能转侧，日久阴变为阳，寒化为热，热甚而腐肉为脓，此疽已成也。凡治此证，初起寒热作痛时，便用五积散加牛膝、红花，发汗散寒，通行经络；或万灵丹发汗亦可。次以大防风汤行经活血，渗湿补虚。又有生于尻臀部位，漫肿作疼者，内托羌活汤；腿内近膝股漫肿木痛者，内托芪柴汤；腿外侧者，内托酒煎汤。初起，通用人参败毒散加木瓜、牛膝、苏木、红花；虚者十全大补汤加羌活、防己、牛膝。已成欲作脓者附子八珍汤。[27p]

Surgical Essentials 【Ming Dynasty, Chen Shigong】

Bone Abscess

Bone abscess, or "Fu Gu Ju," arises from cold and damp invading the bones. However, if a person’s vital energy and blood are robust and healthy, even in the face of cold, malevolent forces cannot penetrate the bones. Those afflicted are generally individuals with weak constitutions, exposed to cold and damp while sleeping in summer and autumn, or those who have had intimate relationships covered with thin bedding, allowing cold air to enter their bodies through weaknesses, ultimately leading to this illness. Initially, symptoms include alternating chills and fever, resembling wind invasions. Subsequently, pain in the buttocks and legs ensues, without significant heat or redness, but with bone-deep pain; in severe cases, the affected cannot move or turn. Over time, the cold transforms into heat, worsening until flesh rots and turns to pus, indicating the abscess has formed.

For treatment, at the onset of chills and fever with pain, employ "Wu Ji San" with added "Niu Xi" and "Hong Hua" to induce sweating, dispel cold, and promote circulation. Alternatively, "Wan Ling Dan" can also be used for sweating. Follow up with "Da Fang Feng Tang" to invigorate blood flow, dispel dampness, and replenish vitality. In cases where the abscess occurs in the buttocks causing diffuse swelling and pain, "Nei Tuo Qiang Huo Tang" should be applied; for diffuse swelling and pain near the knee and thigh, use "Nei Tuo Qi Chai Tang"; and for the outer side of the leg, employ "Nei Tuo Jiu Jian Tang." At the early stage, a universally applicable remedy is "Ren Shen Bai Du San" with added "Mu Guo," "Niu Xi," "Su Mu," and "Hong Hua." For those with deficiency, use "Shi Quan Da Bu Tang" with additions of "Qiang Huo," "Fang Ji," and "Niu Xi." When an abscess is about to form pus, use "Fu Zi Ba Zhen Tang."[27p]

脓成胀痛者即针之，脓稠而黄体实者十全大补汤，脓清色白体虚者保元大成汤，食少体倦者香砂六君子汤，脾虚寒热者补中益气汤，以此调理可也。又有风湿相成之证，初起寒热交作，次传腿肿作痛，其形光亮微红，发热肿痛，按之如泥不便起者，宜当归拈痛汤或茯苓佐经汤，间服万灵丹和之。以上之证，皆由元气不足中来，不可悞用损脾泄气败毒等药，外禁寒凉等法。如悞用之，必致气血冰凝，内肉瘀腐，日久化为污水败脓，流而不禁者，终死。又有房欲劳伤，寒热互变，气血乖违，经脉横解，受病日深，以成斯疾者，其患大腿渐渐肿如冬瓜，上过胯腹，下连足底，牵连漫肿，皮色不红，日久溃脓，色白腥秽，肿仍不消，痛仍不减，元气日衰，身体缩小，唇舌干焦，二便枯秘，诸药不效，饮食不进者，终为不治。　　看法[28p]

For an abscess that has formed with swelling and pain, one should apply acupuncture. For thick yellow pus with a solid body, the formula "Shiquan Dabu Tang" (Ten Complete Great Tonifying Decoction) is appropriate. For clear white pus with a weak body, use "Baoyuan Dacheng Tang" (Great Achievement of Preserving Origin Decoction). For those with little appetite and fatigue, "Xiangsha Liujunzi Tang" (Aromatic Sand Six Gentlemen Decoction) is recommended. For cases of spleen deficiency with alternating cold and heat, "Buzhong Yiqi Tang" (Tonifying the Middle and Augmenting Qi Decoction) is suitable, as these formulas can help regulate the condition.

There are also cases of wind-dampness presenting as initially alternating chills and fevers, followed by leg swelling and pain, characterized by a smooth and slightly red appearance, accompanied by heat and swelling. If pressed, the area feels like mud and is difficult to move; in such instances, "Danggui Nian Tong Tang" (Angelica Pain-Relieving Decoction) or "Fuling Zuojing Tang" (Poria Assisting the Channels Decoction) should be used, intermittently paired with "Wanling Dan" (Universal Cure Pill) to enhance the treatment.

All the above conditions arise from insufficient vital energy and should not be treated with tonics that drain the spleen, expel energy, or weaken toxins, nor should cold and cooling methods be employed externally. Misuse of such treatments will surely lead to stagnant and congealed vital energy and blood, internal flesh becoming necrotic, which over time will turn into foul pus and drain uncontrollably, leading to fatal outcomes.

Furthermore, for those whose condition arises from sexual exhaustion, experiencing alternating cold and heat, disharmony of vital energy and blood, and obstruction of the meridians, which deepens the disease, the affliction may cause the thigh to gradually swell as large as a winter melon, extending from above the hips down to the soles of the feet, resulting in diffuse swelling with skin that is not red. Over time, it may ulcerate with pus that is white and fetid, persisting swelling and unrelenting pain, leading to a decline in vital energy and body mass, with dry and scorched lips and tongue, and hard, secretive excretion. If various medicines are ineffective and food intake ceases, it will ultimately become untreatable.[28p]

　　初起，身微寒热，饮食如常，结肿微红，疼不附骨者，顺。已成，举动自便，结肿成囊，疼痛有时，脓易成者，为吉。已溃，脓稠肿消痛减，身体轻便，苏醒睡稳不热者，吉。溃后，元气易复，饮食易进，内肉易实，脓水易干者，吉。初起，身发寒热，漫肿色白，肢体牵强，疼痛附骨者，险。已成，举动不便，通腿漫肿，不热不红，不作脓者，为险。已溃，脓水清稀，气秽腥臭，肿痛不消，形体日削者，死。溃后，脾胃虚弱，饮食无味，口渴不止，唇白皮枯者，死。　　治法[29p]

At the onset, if there is mild chills and fever, eating and drinking are normal, with slight swelling that is red and pain not reaching the bone, it is considered favorable. Once developed, if movement is easy, swelling forms into a pouch, pain occurs intermittently, and pus easily forms, it is auspicious. After it has burst, if the pus is thick, swelling reduces, pain lessens, the body feels light, and sleep is stable without fever, it is good. After bursting, if vital energy recovers easily, appetite returns quickly, internal flesh reinforces easily, and pus and water dry up easily, it is auspicious.

At the onset, if there are chills and fever, swelling is diffuse and pale in color, limbs are stiff, and pain reaches the bone, it is perilous. Once developed, if movement is inhibited, the leg swells diffusely, neither hot nor red, and does not produce pus, it is dangerous. After bursting, if the pus is thin and watery, with foul-smelling gas, swelling and pain persist, and the body continues to weaken, it is fatal. After bursting, if the spleen and stomach are weak, with no taste in food, persistent thirst, pale lips, and dry skin, it is fatal.

Treatment methods.[29p]

　　初起，发热恶寒，身体拘急，腿脚肿痛，脉浮紧者，宜散之。已成，腿脚肿痛，皮色不变，上下通肿者，宜散寒温经络；寒热作肿，色白光亮，按之如泥不起者，宜健脾渗湿；身体无热，恶寒脉迟而濇，腿肿不热者，宜养血温经络；暑中三阴，脉洪而数，腿脚焮肿，口干便燥者，宜下之。已溃，脓水清稀，饮食减少，形体消瘦者，宜补中健脾胃。溃后，肿痛不减，脓水不止，虚热不退者，宜温中养气血。愈后，筋骨牵强，曲伸不便者，宜滋养气血，通利关节。[30p]

At the onset, with fever and chills, a tight body, and swollen painful legs, the condition should be dispersed. Once established, with swollen painful legs and unchanged skin color, swelling throughout the body should be treated by dispersing cold and warming the meridians. If swelling is caused by alternating cold and heat, the affected area is white and shiny and feels soft like mud when pressed, the focus should be on strengthening the spleen and promoting fluid metabolism. If there is no fever, chills with a slow and thin pulse, and leg swelling without heat, one should nourish the blood and warm the meridians. In cases of summer heat with a rapid and strong pulse, swollen legs, dry mouth, and constipation, treatment should be about purgation. After the condition has erupted and there is clear, thin pus, decreased appetite, and weight loss, one should strengthen the middle and bolster the spleen and stomach. If, after eruption, swelling and pain persist, with continuous pus and unresolved deficiency heat, one should warm the middle and nourish qi and blood. After recovery, if there are tightness in the muscles and joints making bending and stretching difficult, one should nourish qi and blood to promote joint mobility.[30p]

　　　　景岳全书 【明　张介宾】

　　　　　附骨证论治

　　附骨疽一证，近俗呼为贴骨痈。凡疽毒最深而结聚于骨际者，皆可谓之附骨疽。然尤惟两股间肉厚处乃多此证。盖此证之因，有劳伤筋骨而残损其脉者，有恃酒力房而因烁其阴者，有忧思郁怒而留结其气者，有风邪寒湿而凑滞其经者。凡人于环跳穴处，无故酸痛久而不愈者，便是此证之兆，速当因证调治，不可迟也。盖其初起，不过少阳经一点逆滞，逆而不散，则以渐而壅，壅则肿，肿则溃；至其延漫，则三阴三阳，无不连及，而全腿俱溃。然此证无非元气大亏，不能运行，故致留滞不散，而后致决裂，诚危证也。若溃后脉和，虽见困弱之甚，只以大补气血为主，皆可保全。若溃后脉反洪芤，而烦躁不宁，发热口渴，则必不可治。至若治此之法，凡以劳伤筋骨而致者，宜大营煎兼大防风汤治之。[31p]

Complete Book of Jingyue by Zhang Jieben (Ming Dynasty)

Discussion on Appendicular Bone Abscess Treatment

The condition known as appendicular bone abscess is commonly referred to in modern terms as a bone abscess. Any abscess caused by deep toxic energy gathering at the bone interface can be termed as such. However, this condition particularly occurs in the thicker flesh between the thighs. The causes of this condition include injuries to the muscles and bones resulting in damage to the blood vessels, excessive indulgence in alcohol leading to depletion of the body's Yin, emotional distress and anger causing stagnation of Qi, and invasion by wind, cold, and dampness that obstructs the meridians. If a person experiences prolonged and unexplained soreness at the Hui Tiao point, it is a sign of this condition, and urgent treatment is necessary.

Initially, it arises from a slight blockage in the Shaoyang meridian; if this blockage does not resolve, it gradually leads to obstruction, swelling, and potential rupture. As it spreads, it affects all three Yin and three Yang meridians, leading to overall leg disruption. This condition fundamentally results from a significant depletion of the vital energy, causing stagnation that can lead to rupture, making it a serious condition.

If rupture occurs and the pulse is harmonious, although the patient may feel extremely weak, focusing on replenishing Qi and blood can ensure recovery. However, if after rupture the pulse is forceful and wiry, coupled with restlessness, fever, and thirst, then treatment is not advised. For treatment of this condition resulting from injury to muscles and bones, it is recommended to use a combination of the Da Ying Decoction and the Da Fang Feng Decoction.[31p]

若酒色伤阴者，宜八味丸、六味丸或右归丸兼大防风汤主之。若忧思郁怒结气者，宜疮科流气饮或五香连翘汤，兼大防风汤主之。若风寒外袭者，宜五积散兼大防风汤主之。大抵此证初起，即宜用大营煎温补气血，或兼仙方活命饮通行毒气。有火者，宜速用连翘归尾煎以解散其毒，仍宜速用隔蒜灸或豆豉饼寻头灸之，以速散其毒，最为捷法。其有湿热痰饮等证，当并求后法以治之，庶免大害也。若环跳久痛不已，或见臀股微肿，度其已成，势不能散，只宜速用托补，专固根本，使其速起速溃，则根本既实，虽凶亦无大害，必且易溃易敛而易愈也。若脉见滑数，按之软熟，脓已成也，速宜针之，无使久留，以防深入之患。其有不明利害，苟图目前，或用克伐消散再伤元气，或用寒凉敷药以遏其毒气，以致日延日甚，而元气日败，则一溃不可收拾矣。考诸方书，俱未详及此证，故悉其所因，并附治案。[32p]

If alcohol or excessive emotions harm the body’s Yin, one should use Ba Wei Wan, Liu Wei Wan, or You Gui Wan along with Da Fang Feng Decoction. If anxiety, worry, or anger cause qi stagnation, one should use Chuang Ke Liu Qi Drink or Wu Xiang Lian Qiao Decoction combined with Da Fang Feng Decoction. If attacked by wind-cold from outside, one should use Wu Ji San combined with Da Fang Feng Decoction. Generally, if this condition arises, one should promptly use Da Ying Decoction to warm and tonify qi and blood, or combine it with Xian Fang Huo Ming Drink to expel toxins.

In cases of heat, one should quickly use Lian Qiao Gui Wei Decoction to resolve the toxins, and also quickly apply garlic moxibustion or bean paste cakes for direct moxibustion to rapidly disperse the toxins, which is the most effective method. If there are symptoms of damp-heat or phlegm accumulation, further treatment methods should be sought to avoid serious harm.

If there is persistent pain at the环跳 point or slight swelling in the hip and thigh, and it is judged to have formed, one must act quickly to nourish and strengthen the root, facilitating a quick rupture; if the base is solid, even if there are serious issues, the harm will be minimized, and it will be easier for it to burst, gather, and heal. If the pulse is slippery and rapid, pressing indicates it is soft and ripe, indicating pus formation; it is urgent to use acupuncture to prevent it from being retained for too long and causing deeper issues.

If one is unclear about the benefits and harms, pursuing immediate relief might involve methods that harm the root qi, or using cold and cooling medicines to suppress the toxic qi, leading to prolonged suffering and weakening of the root qi; this would result in an inevitable, uncontrollable rupture. Texts have not thoroughly detailed these conditions, so the underlying causes and treatment strategies are compiled.[32p]

　　　　方

　　疮科流气饮　治阴发流注，恚怒气结，堆核肿硬作痛；或胸膈痞闷；或风寒湿毒，搏于经络；或血不和，结成肿块，肉色不变；或漫肿木闷无头；或阴发乳岩等证，未成速散，已成速溃，败脓自出，恶肉自去，非常之验。　　桔梗　人参　当归　桂　甘草　黄芪盐水炒　厚朴姜制　紫苏　白芍药　乌药　防风　枳壳　槟榔　南木香　川芎　白芷　　右，生姜煎服。疼痛加乳香、没药，疮干加知母、贝母，疮不干加炒皂角刺，流注加羌活、独活，气滞加香附，胃虚加陈皮。此乃行气散血之剂，若服之过度，则气血虚耗，何以为脓？学者知之。[33p]

Prescription

For treating sores with flowing Qi: This remedy addresses fluid retention resulting from internal heat, emotional stagnation, or accumulations that cause hard, painful lumps; it may also alleviate chest fullness or dampness from wind and cold, affecting the meridians; or blood stagnation forming lumps that remain a normal color; or widespread swelling that is heavy without a clear starting point; or symptoms like yin deficiency and lumps akin to breasts, whether they are beginning to fester or have already developed pus with unhealthy tissue.

Ingredients: Platycodon, ginseng, angelica, cinnamon, licorice, astragalus (fried in salt water), magnolia bark (prepared with ginger), perilla, white peony, lindera, saposhnikovia, bitter orange, betel palm, fragrant wood, chuanxiong, and angelica dahurica.

Direction: Boil with fresh ginger for oral consumption. For pain, add frankincense and myrrh; if the sore is dry, add anemarrhena and fritillaria; if not dry, add fried soapberry spikes; for fluid retention, include qinghao and duhuo; for Qi stagnation, add cyperus; for stomach deficiency, use aged tangerine peel. This is a formula for invigorating Qi and dispersing blood. If taken excessively, it may harm Qi and blood, leading to insufficient material for pus formation. Scholars should be aware of this.[33p]

　　败毒流气饮　治流注初发，堆核硬痛，不可忍，用此疏邪流气。　　羌活　独活　青木香　赤芍药　当归　紫苏　陈皮　香附　白芷　三棱　蓬莪朮　枳壳　川芎　桔梗　柴胡　半夏姜制　赤茯苓　甘草　　右，生姜煎服。热加大黄、黄芩，虚加人参、黄芪。
　　方脉流气饮　治阴发流注瘰疬，及郁结肿聚结块，或走注疼痛，或心胸痞闷，胁腹胀满，呕吐不食，上气喘急，咳嗽痰盛，或面目四肢浮肿，大小便秘者。　　紫苏　青皮　白芍药　当归　白茯苓　乌药　桔梗炒　半夏姜制　黄芪炒　川芎　枳实炒　陈皮　防风　南木香　大腹皮　甘草　槟榔　枳壳　　右，生姜煎服。流注加羌活、独活、白芷梢，小便不通加木通、栀子，浮肿加猪苓、泽泻，气滞加香附，血滞加肉桂，呕吐加藿香，瘰疬加夏枯草。此行气耗血之剂，不过二三剂止之，不可多服。[34p]

Baiduliuqi Decoction
Used to treat the initial onset of flowing heat, hard lumps causing unbearable pain, and to dispel evil flowing Qi. Ingredients: Qianghuo, Duhuo, Qingmuxiang, Chishao, Danggui, Zisu, Chenpi, Xiangfu, Baizhi, Sanleng, Pengaozhu, Zhike, Chuanxiong, Jiegeng, Chaihu, Banxia (prepared with ginger), Chihongling, Gancao. Decoction with fresh ginger. For heat, add Dahuang and Huangqin; for deficiency, add Renshen and Huangqi.

Fangmai Liuqi Decoction
Used to treat Ying-type flowing lymph nodes, as well as stagnation, swelling, and masses; symptoms like pain from moving pus, chest and heart discomfort, abdominal fullness, vomiting, anorexia, shortness of breath with wheezing, coughing with excessive phlegm, or localized swelling in the face and limbs, with constipation. Ingredients: Zisu, Qingpi, Baishao, Danggui, Baifuling, Wuyao, Jiegeng (stir-fried), Banxia (prepared with ginger), Huangqi (stir-fried), Chuanxiong, Zhishi (stir-fried), Chenpi, Fangfeng, Nanmuxiang, Dafuzi, Gancao, Biting, Zhike. Decoction with fresh ginger. For flowing pus, add Qianghuo, Duhuo, Baizhi tips; for urinary obstruction, add Muwutong and Zhizhi; for swelling, add Zhuling and Zexie; for Qi stagnation, add Xiangfu; for blood stagnation, add Rougui; for vomiting, add Huoxiang; for lymph nodes, add Xiakucao. This is a formula to move Qi and nourish blood, typically should not exceed two to three doses. Avoid overuse.[34p]

Miao Cao San - for treating initial symptoms.

Neisai San - for treating yin deficiency and yang qi attacking causing swelling, or erupting without healing, or wind-cold attacking the affected area, leading to inability of qi and blood to circulate, often resulting in a chronic condition.
Take Fuzi soaked in several bowls of boy’s urine for three days and nights, cut into four pieces, soak again for several days and nights, replacing the urine daily. Prepare with:
Cinamomum (Guiling), red mung beans, honey-fried licorice, Astragalus (decocted in salt water and stir-fried), Angelica (blended with wine), Fuling, Bai Zhi, and Jie Geng (stir-fried), Chuanxiong (prepared), Yuan Zhi (pitted), Houpoke (made with ginger), and Ren Shen, each 1 liang; Fang Feng 4 qian.

　　黄狗下颏方　治肚痈少腹痈，及腿上贴骨痈，神效。又云可治发背。大抵此方治下部痈疽妙。　　黄狗下颏连舌遵皮毛劈下，入罐盐泥封固，铁盏盖口，煅一炷香，烟觉清即止，务宜存性，不可过，遇则无用矣。视其骨灰正黑色者为妙。若带白色，其性已过，勿用。用时研极细　白蔹末　生豌豆粉　　右三味等分，以各五钱为率，酒调空腹服；外又以三味等分为敷药，香油调敷患处。其验以服药后出臭汗及熟睡为准。史鹤亭太史，亲见顾天宇室人验过。　　按此方世多用之。万氏家抄，亦已收载。然但知其可为敷药，散肿止痛，而不知其可以内服，为下部痈疽内消之圣药也。予有轿夫，环跳穴痛甚如鸡啄火灼，适制有药，以酒调三钱饮之，未愈，更进一服，霍然如失，明日舁轿如故，了无苦矣。[39p]

The yellow dog's lower jaw is a remedy for abdominal and lower abdominal carbuncles, as well as bone carbuncles on the legs, with remarkable effects. It is also said to be able to treat back ailments. Generally, this remedy is excellent for treating lower body sores and boils.

Take the yellow dog's lower jaw and tongue, together with the skin and fur, and chop it finely. Place it in a jar with salt and clay, sealing it tightly with an iron lid. Burn a stick of incense; when the smoke becomes clear, stop. It is important to maintain the right properties, as over-processing will render it ineffective. The ash should be purely black to be considered effective; if it has white, it has been over-processed and should not be used. When preparing, grind it into a very fine powder.

Mix equal parts of the coarse powder, including white mustache powder and fresh pea powder; each should be five qian (a traditional weight unit). Take it on an empty stomach with wine. Externally, use equal parts of the three ingredients as a poultice, mixed with fragrant oil and applied to the affected area. The effectiveness can be judged by the appearance of foul-smelling sweat and deep sleep after taking the medicine.

The historian He Ting observed the effects firsthand when visiting Gu Tianyu's residence. Many in the world have used this remedy, and it has been recorded in the Wan family's manuscript. However, they only recognize its use as a poultice to reduce swelling and alleviate pain, without realizing that it is a miraculous drug for internal consumption to eliminate lower body sores and boils. I once had a litter carrier who experienced severe pain in his lower back, as if being pecked by a chicken or burned by fire. I happened to have this medicine and mixed three qian with wine for him to drink. He did not improve after the first dose, but after taking a second dose, he suddenly felt relief. The next day, he carried the litter as usual, without any pain left.[39p]

　　三生散　治诸疮大痛，不辨肉色，漫肿光色，名附骨痈，如神。　　露蜂房　蛇退　头发洗净，各等分

　　内托黄芪柴胡汤　治附骨痈。
　　黄芪二钱　柴胡　土瓜根酒洗净，各一钱　羌活半钱　连翘一钱三分　官桂　黄蘗　生地黄各二分　当归七分半　　右(口父)咀，作一服，水一盏，酒一盏，同煎至一盏，去滓热服，宿食消尽，一服而愈。昔贾德茂男年十岁，丁未四月十一日，于左腿近膝股内出附骨痈，不辨肉色，漫肿，皮泽木硬，疮势甚大。其左脚乃肝之脾土也，原在足厥阴肝经之分，少侵足太阴脾经之分，其脉左部细而弦，按之缓而微有力，为制此方主治。一方无黄蘗。[40p]

San Sheng San: Treats severe pain from various sores, where the flesh color is indiscernible and the swelling has a glossy appearance, known as "attached bone abscess," resembling a divine condition.

Lu Feng Fang: After washing the hair clean, take equal parts of the following: burn to ash and keep the essence, grind finely, and consume three qian with wine.

Nei Tuo Huang Qi Chai Hu Decoction: Treats attached bone abscess.
Ingredients: 2 qian Huang Qi, 1 qian each of Chai Hu and Tu Gua Gen (cleaned with wine), 0.5 qian Qiang Huo, 1.3 qian Lian Qiao, 0.2 qian each of Guan Gui, Huang Bo, and Sheng Di Huang, 0.75 qian Dang Gui.

Crush the above ingredients together to make one dose. Boil in one cup of water and one cup of wine until reduced to one cup, then strain and take while hot. It will help with the digestion of overnight food, and one dose will cure the condition.

In the past, Jia De Mao's son, aged ten years, developed an attached bone abscess on April 11 of the Ding Wei year, near the knee on the inner thigh of the left leg, where the flesh color was indiscernible, with swelling and skin appearing wooden and hard, presenting a significant sore. The left foot corresponds to the liver and spleen, originally located in the foot's jueyin liver channel, slightly encroaching upon the foot's taiyin spleen channel. His pulse on the left side was fine and wiry, pressing slowly revealed a slight strength, leading to the formulation of this prescription. One ingredient was missing, Huang Bo.[40p]

　　内托黄芪酒煎汤
　　黄芪　当归尾各二钱　柴胡一钱半　连翘　肉桂　鼠粘子炒，各一钱　升麻七分　黄蘗　炙甘草各半钱　　右(口父)咀，好糯米酒一盏，水一大盏半，同煎至一大盏，去滓，空心，宿食消尽温服，待少时，早膳压之，使不令大热上攻中上二焦也。丁未季春蒲度主老，年七十，因寒湿地气，得附骨疽于左腿外侧足少阳胆经之分，微侵足阳明分，阔六七寸，长一尺，坚硬漫肿，不辨肉色，皮泽深，但行步作痛，以指按至骨大痛，与药一服，立止；再服，坚硬肿消。[41p]

Internal decoction of astragalus wine

Astragalus, two qian; angelica tail, two qian; bupleurum, one and a half qian; forsythia, one qian; cinnamon, one qian; processed mouse glue, one qian; ligusticum, seven fen; yellow bristle, half qian; roasted licorice, half qian.

Combine these ingredients, add one cup of good glutinous rice wine and one and a half large cups of water, and decoct until reduced to one large cup. Strain, take on an empty stomach, after all food has digested and warmed, wait a little while, and take with breakfast to prevent excessive heat from rising and attacking the middle and upper jiao.

In the late spring of Ding Wei, a patient named Pu Du, aged seventy, suffered from bone abscess on the outer side of the left leg, in the foot's lesser yang gallbladder channel, slightly encroaching on the foot's yangming area, with a size of six to seven inches wide and one foot long. It was hard, swollen, and difficult to discern the color of the flesh, with deep skin texture. Walking caused pain and pressing with a finger led to severe pain in the bone. After taking the medicine once, it stopped immediately; after taking it again, the hardness and swelling diminished.[41p]

Danggui Powder: Treats bone abscesses and all kinds of malignant sores.
Ingredients: 1.5 taels of Angelica Sinensis, 12 dried gardenias, 1 dried prickly ash (shelled), 1 tael of licorice. Grind all into a fine powder. Take 9 grams mixed with cool wine.

Luo Lu Decoction: Treats bone carbuncles.
Ingredients: 1 tael of peeled reed roots, 1 tael of Cimicifuga, 1 tael of Forsythia, 1 tael of Ephedra (roots removed), 0.5 tael each of Stephania, Saussurea, White Poria, and Sandalwood, and 1.5 taels of prepared rhubarb (fried). Crush all together. For each dose, take 15 grams with 1.5 cups of water, add 7 pieces of bamboo leaves, boil until reduced by a third, add 3 grams of Glauber's salt, mix well, strain, and take warm on an empty stomach. If the effect is not sufficient, take again.

Ying Tong Pills: Treats sudden pain, suspected to be bone abscess.
Ingredients: 1 tael each of Atractylodes (peeled), Angelica Sinensis, Black Morning Glory, and processed Aconite. Grind these into a fine powder, mix with vinegar to form pills the size of small beans. Take 30 pills with sour soup on an empty stomach.[42p]
